text-align--left__373c0__2XGa-"><span class="lemon--span__373c0__3997G raw__373c0__3rKqk" lang="en">SC and I got take out from here for a &#34;fancy night in.&#34; We placed our orders online (picked one app, entree, and dessert/ person) and went to pick up with ease. Overall, it was a tasty dinner. It definitely would&#39;ve been better eating it fresh/ at the restaurant since a lot of the textural elements got soft/ disappeared in the process of taking it home, but that&#39;s to be expected and certainly not fault of the restaurant.<br><br>Apps:<br>- Spring Asparagus Soup: <br>curry / pickled onion / coconut milk / ginger / crispy shallot<br>Really light, full of asparagus flavor. Missed the crispiness of the shallots<br>- Mushroom Risotto:<br>shiitake / crimini / parmesan crisp / truffle oil<br>Loved the variety of mushrooms. Missed the crispiness of the parm<br><br>Entrees:<br>- Seafood Bouillabaisse:<br>salmon / shrimp / scallop / mussels / tomato / thai lobster broth<br>Didn&#39;t see any scallops in the soup but had 4 mussels, 3 shrimp and a big chunk of salmon along with tomatoes and fennel (?). The soup didn&#39;t have a ton of flavor (mostly tasted like salmon to me) but I did appreciate the variety of seafood in there and it was delicious with bread<br>- Diver Scallops:<br>butternut squash purée / brussels sprouts / bacon marmalade<br>Our favorite dish. The scallops were cooked beautifully and all the flavors married so well together. I especially loved the bacon marmalade. Missed the crispiness of the sprouts<br><br>Dessert:<br>- Cheese Plate:<br>Manchego / Gruyère / Délice de Crémiers / with baguette / candied walnuts / honey / fig jam<br>Didn&#39;t receive any fig jam (we had our own tho!) There was A TON of bread (which we also ate with the bouillabaisse above). We toasted the bread at home because it had gotten soggy en route. Couldn&#39;t decipher any flavors from the walnuts; I assume it was meant to be a crunchy element. There was also some accompanying berries which was nice.  The cheeses were good, though SC thought the Delice was a little too funky for him.<br>- Vegan Coconut Panna Cotta:<br>coconut milk / toasted coconut / fresh berries<br>Also came with a coconut roll that unfortunately got crushed in the container. I missed the crunchiness of it and the toasted coconut but I enjoyed the combination of the flavors. The pannna cotta was well set and still smooth and creamy.</span></p></div><div class="lemon--div__373c0__1mboc margin-t3__373c0__1l90z margin-b2__373c0__abANL class="lemon--p__373c0__3Qnnj text__373c0__2Kxyz comment__373c0__3EKjH text-color--normal__373c0__3xep9 text-align--left__373c0__2XGa-"><span class="lemon--span__373c0__3997G raw__373c0__3rKqk" lang="en">Trendy new American restaurant serving seasonally and globally inspired dishes at high price points. Prices are high not just for Ann Arbor, but even compared to NYC, and I don&#39;t think it&#39;s entirely reflected in the quality. As a Google maps review says, `They claim that it&#39;s &#34;local&#34; yet no mention of the farms they get their food from. Which makes me believe it&#39;s another restaurant using &#34;local&#34; for marketing.&#39; Spencer is a much better option for seasonal new American in the $$$ range.<br><br>Disclaimer: I wasn&#39;t very hungry so I only got an appetizer and tried some desserts.<br><br>Most of my friends said they were happy with their entrees, though one said his perch was overcooked and overpriced. The desserts are definitely overpriced for what they are, and they&#39;re plated in a very unappealing way. I tried:<br><br>Mussels ($15) - the mussels themselves were quite large and plump, and they were cooked well. The white wine broth was extremely salty, and the bread for dipping was mediocre (and wasn&#39;t offered to be refilled. and it wasn&#39;t grilled).<br><br>Lemon meringue ($11): it&#39;s some messily piped lemon curd (not a semifreddo as shown in others&#39; pictures) on a plate topped with roasted meringue. The meringue texture was weird and lumpy. The lemon curd was extremely sweet, and the entire dessert was very soft and felt unbalanced. The presentation was also quite bad.<br><br>Coconut panna cotta ($10) - the taste was quite good but the portion was laughably tiny. The texture was more on the firm side for panna cotta.<br><br>Chocolate bodino squares ($11) - the taste was pretty good but nothing spectacular.<br><br>Service was mostly normal. Our server fake cried when we asked to split the bill, which was weird. There&#39;s an automatic 20% gratuity for large parties.</span></p></div><div class="lemon--div__373c0__1mboc margin-t3__373c0__1l90z margin-b2__373c0__abANL border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><div class="lemon--div__373c0__1mboc photo-box-grid__373c0__1C3ha border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><span class="lemon--span__373c0__3997G photo-box-grid-item__373c0__2kFqV display--inline__373c0__3JqBP border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><div class="lemon--div__373c0__1mboc on-click-container border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><a class="lemon--a__373c0__IEZFH link__373c0__1G70M photo-box-link__373c0__1YC9Y link-color--blue-dark__373c0__85-Nu link-size--default__373c0__7tls6" href="/biz_photos/taste-kitchen-ann-arbor?reviewid=69sczYN8mttSiBFNvuM2YA&amp;select=PDvKleew48wadj9cZuATIA" target="" name="" rel=""><img class="lemon--img__373c0__3GQUb photo-box-img__373c0__35y5v" src="https://s3-media0.fl.yelpcdn.com/bphoto/PDvKleew48wadj9cZuATIA/348s.jpg" alt="Photo of Taste Kitchen - Ann Arbor, MI, United States. text-align--left__373c0__2XGa-"><span class="lemon--span__373c0__3997G raw__373c0__3rKqk" lang="en">Yum! We had reservations for a Friday night during Michigan&#39;s move in weekend, and were seated right away. It was very busy in the restaurant, which is always a good sign. <br><br>Our waiter was very knowledgeable and answered all of our questions about the wine list. I tried a new wine that I enjoyed! They also have unique cocktails, which looked good enough that I had to order one after my glass of wine, and it did not disappoint. <br><br>For food, we shared a cheese plate (great variety of cheeses). They made sure to refill our bread, which was thoughtful. Two of us were also brave enough to try the octopus, which had a delicious flavor but I&#39;m not sure either of us could get over eating octopus! <br><br>For dinner, we tried the oven roasted salmon, which was on a delicious cauliflower purée with salsa verde and some veggies. Two of us got the grilled Berkshire pork, which - wow - AMAZING. It comes with Brussels sprouts which could have easily been the star of the show, they were that good. The pork was cooked perfectly, sat on a bed of rice, and a fried egg was on top - that made for a delicious meal. <br><br>The three of us shared the lemon meringue for dessert, which was the perfect combination of sour and sweet. It even won this anti-sweet things person over - I thought it was delicious!<br><br>Overall, this place was great. The atmosphere is fun and full of energy, the food was delicious, and the drinks were good. Great location - it&#39;s close to a parking garage and everything downtown Ann Arbor has to offer!</span></p></div><div class="lemon--div__373c0__1mboc margin-t3__373c0__1l90z margin-b2__373c0__abANL border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><div class="lemon--div__373c0__1mboc photo-box-grid__373c0__1C3ha border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><span class="lemon--span__373c0__3997G photo-box-grid-item__373c0__2kFqV display--inline__373c0__3JqBP border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><div class="lemon--div__373c0__1mboc on-click-container border-color--default__373c0__3-ifU"><a class="lemon--a__373c0__IEZFH link__373c0__1G70M photo-box-link__373c0__1YC9Y link-color--blue-dark__373c0__85-Nu link-size--default__373c0__7tls6" href="/biz_photos/taste-kitchen-ann-arbor?reviewid=gQGp-KBOMPnGy-UmS_-uzw&amp;select=JzFH6HlryIIJvfTRhYFYCA" target="" name="" rel=""><img class="lemon--img__373c0__3GQUb photo-box-img__373c0__35y5v" src="https://s3-media0.fl.yelpcdn.com/bphoto/JzFH6HlryIIJvfTRhYFYCA/348s.jpg" alt="Photo of Taste Kitchen - Ann Arbor, MI, United States. lang="en">Came here for dinner while in town and was super impressed. Clearly a popular spot as it filled up quickly, and everything was well thought out, from instagrammable cocktails to impeccably decorated dishes. We grabbed the cheese plate to share, which was good but nothing too special, as well as the octopus and mussels. These were delicious - the octopus was very lightly fried and just right, with great flavor, and the mussels were in a rich tomato-based sauce that was incredible. Plenty of grilled bread to mop up the sauce - so good. Instead of an entree I opted for two of the small plates - the beet salad and shrimp risotto. Both were amazing, honestly. The shrimp risotto was packed with shrimp, different mushrooms, and cheese crisps - super rich, and the sugary beets paired well with the walnuts/goat cheese. Ended the meal with the chocolate bodino squares, which were almost fudge-like in consistency - so good, with delicious raspberry coulis and brandy whipped cream. Great service throughout, and everything was amazing. and it was my bday.<br><br>My friends and I had to wait a while to be seated. I would recommend a max of 6 people per group for this restaurant. We had to wait for two tables to turn before we could be seated, which wasn&#39;t very efficient. However, we were able to get alcohol at the bar and chill. The restaurant is a little crowded and small, so there wasn&#39;t a true waiting area, and I felt bad for the people whose seats we were brushed up against. Lastly, a friend had to leave in the middle of dinner and several others skipped their secondary plans for the evening because we were seated so late, which wasn&#39;t cool.<br><br>FOOD:<br>The Boullibaisse was delicious. The shrimp and scallop were perfectly cooked. There wasn&#39;t a ton of seafood in the soup though (+4 mussels).<br><br>Fillet mignon was good, but I think one of my friends went home a little hungry. Maybe we should&#39;ve ordered more? But a $65 meal (including alcohol) is already pretty $$$. <br><br>SERVICE:<br>Phenomenal and attentive. I accidentally spilled my red wine while talking to someone and I turned to see napkins arrive immediately at the table and my friend was offered club soda (luckily she was wearing dark clothes).
